et saiches que li jointure n’iert jamais fichie en son leu.	and know that the joint will never be fixed in its place.
Li dislocation qui est devers lou pis, et les mameles, ou derrier, si est faite par impulsion, et estendement de mains, et i aministre on autre lieure;	The dislocation that is toward the worst, and the joints, either front or back, are caused by a sudden movement, extending the hands, and similar actions, and require another treatment.
et cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and heal as long as he is healthy.
Et se aprés la sanation vient grietez au membre, et tardemens em movement, si use li malaides bain maintes fois, tant que celle grietez soit alegie, et reviegne a sa premiere nature.	And after healing comes cracking in the limb, and delayed movement; if the patient uses it often enough, as long as that cracking is relieved, and returns to its original state.
de la dislocation dou coute	of the dislocation cost
Saiches que li jointure dou coute est desaluee a poinnes, et a poinnes revient;	Knowing that the joint's pain is caused by dislocation, and it repeatedly dislocates;
et s’est desaluee de toutes pars, et meismement devant et derrier, et li dislocations n’est mie reponue, car on la voit bien et sent bien;	and it is dislocated from all sides, especially in front and behind, and the dislocation is not fully corrected, for one can both see and feel it clearly;
et desalue selonc chescune figure.	and dislocated according to each misalignment.
Et quant tu joins le coute malaide avec lou sain, si le pues veoir apertement.	And when you join the sick part with the healthy, if you can see it clearly.
Car li jointure est chevee, et ne puet ploier lou bras, ne touchier son espaule a tout.	Because the joint is dislocated, and the arm cannot bend, nor can it touch the shoulder at all.
Et covient que tu le ramoinnes ainsois que apostemes chaus i viegne, car se apostemes chaus i venoit, si seroit grief li ramener;	And you must reset it so that the dislocation is corrected before it returns, because if the dislocation comes back again, it will be difficult to correct.
et par aventure ne puet estre ramenez dou tout en tout, meismement quant ele est au derrier;	and it may not be brought back completely, especially when it is at the back.
si vaut pis que les autres dislocations, et est de plus grant dolor, et par aventure i vient li mors.	it is worse than other dislocations, causing greater pain, and in some cases it can lead to death.
Et li restauration si est, quant elle est telz c’on la puet ramener, que tu li estendes sa main a tes II mains;	And for the restoration, when it is such that it can be brought back, you should extend your hand with both of yours.
et ses bras soit espandus, et les mains dou mire selonc le coute entor, desor et desoz, et boute la jointure a ses peuchas ensamble, ou a la racine de sa palme, tant qu’ele reviegne a son leu.	And let his arms be spread out, and the hands with wide open fingers according to the contour of the bone around, apart and together, and straighten the joint at his palm's base, until it returns to its place.
Et se li dislocations est au devant, si revient quant il double sa main a sa main, et fier de la racine de la palme lou coute qui est desaluez.	And if the dislocation is at the front, it returns when he doubles his hand to his palm, and turns the root of the palm side that is misaligned.
Et s’il ne vuet revenir au leu, si aministre fort extension;	And if it does not want to return to its place, apply strong extension.
et est que dui ministre estendent le bras, et le teignent dui ministre, si qu’il ne se mueve a l’estension;	and it is that the two ministers extend the arm, and the tie of the two ministers, so that it does not move with the extension.
puis torne le bras de chescune part, puis que tu as envoloupeit un drapeil double lonc et large;	then turn the arm from each side, after you have wrapped a long and wide cloth around it.
et quant li mires a jointe la jointure a sa main, si l’oigne d’aucun oile por amolir la jointure, puis boute la jointure forment, tant qu’ele reviegne;	and when the mirror shows the joint of the joint in the hand, if it is not oiled to soften the joint, then press the joint firmly, until it returns.
et quant elle est au leu, si met sus emplaustre sec avec aubun d’uef, et l’estrain forment, et pent le bras au col dou malaide, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le deslie.	and when it is in place, apply dry plaster with heat and stretch the joint, pressing the arm against the collarbone of the afflicted person, and leave it for no days, then release it.
Et se li jointure est ferme en son leu, si deslie lou liien, et le laisse;	And if the joint is firm in its place, release the ligature, and leave it.
et se tu vois que li jointure n’estrigne bien, si rencomence l’emplaustre et lou lien, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit fermement mis;	and if you see that the joint is not well aligned, recommence the binding and the bandage, and leave it thus for no more than a few days, until it is firmly set.
puis le deslie.	then loosen it.
Et se il sent grieteit aprés le ramenement de la jointe, et elle se muet, si le baigne et frote bellement, et presse tant qu’il soit assouagiez;	and if it feels sore after resetting the joint, and it becomes stiff, then bathe and gently rub it, pressing until it is relieved.
ou tu met sus la jointure une naige de mouton grasse, puis la laisse I jor et une nuit, puis l’oste, et lou fai entrer ou bain;	or place on the joint a greasy sheep fat, leave it there for a day and a night, then remove it, and make the patient take a bath.
et quant il sue, se li frote la jointure tempreement, puis remet la naige sus, et puis entre ou bain;	and when it swells, rub the affected joint tempermentally, then place a cold compress on top, and then immerse it in water.
et ensi fai II fois ou III, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do this twice or three times, as long as it remains healthy;
et se tu vues, si met sus fien de vaiche moiste chaufeit avec burre, et l’estrain sus;	and if you see that it is covered with moist, hot pus and swollen, apply a fine cloth dipped in butter and press it on;
si revenra a sa disposition.	it will return to its original position.
li dislocation de la main	The dislocation of the hand
Li jointure de la main desalue, et li revenue est legiere, plus que les autres jointures.	The joint of the hand dislocates easily, and its return is light, more so than other joints.
Toutevoie, il la covient ramener au leu hastanment, en l’oure meisme qu’ele est desaluee, ainsois que li leus soit enflez, ou qu’il i viegne aposteme chaut.	However, it is necessary to reset it gently in the same moment it dislocates, so that the joint does not swell or an abscess forms hot.
Et li ramenemens si est que tu mettes la main malaide sus une tauble, et estende li ministres la main, et li mires la mette igal, ensi que il mette sa paume sus l’aparance de la jointure, et la boute tant qu’elle reviegne.	And the resetting is done by placing the patient's hand on a table, extending the affected limb, and visually ensuring it aligns evenly; then pressing down on the palm until the joint returns to its place.
Toutevoie, il covient que vos regardez s’il est bien a leu;	However, you should check if it is well-positioned.
adonc mette li malaides lou dos de sa main sus une tauble a l’estension et au ramenement.	Then, place the patient's hand on a table with the fingers extended and then bent.
Et se li dislocations est au dos de la main, si mette li malaides son dos de sa main sus la tauble, et li mires mette sa main sus cele apparance de la jointure.	And if the dislocation is on the back of the hand, let the patient lay his sick hand on a table, and look carefully at the appearance of the joint.
S’elle revient maintenant, c’est bien.	If it returns now, that is good.
Se ce non, si l’estrain d’emplaustres apaisans apostemes chaus, et lou laisse ensi sens rencomencier.	If it does not return, strain soothing plasters over the abscesses, and leave them thus without beginning again.
Et s’il ne le puet soffrir, et tu ne la pues mettre au leu aprés aucuns jors, si demore li jointure torte;	And if he cannot endure it, and you cannot put it back in place after any number of days, then the twisted joint persists.
et ne nuist niant au malaide fuer que tant que li mains est amoillie, et ne puet estraindre aucune chose a tout:	and do not harm the patient until their hands are relaxed, and they cannot squeeze anything at all.
adonc saiches que li nerf sont copez, ou li artere;	so know that the nerves or arteries are cut,
si n’i a autre engien fuer que d’estraindre par cautere delez le cas, et par aventure n’i vaut autre chose.	if there is no other engine but to extract with delicate cautery, and by chance it is worth nothing else.
Et quant li mains est au leu, si met sus l’emplaustre que nos avons dit, puis l’estrain et le laisse V jors, puis le deslie et laisse ensi.	And when the hand is in place, if you put on the plaster as we have said, then pull it and leave it for a day, then loosen it and leave it so.
Et s’il ne la puet bien movoir, et il i a aucune grieteit, si la moille d’aigue chaude, et le frote tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if he cannot move it well, and there is no fracture, then apply warm water and rub it until it is healed.
de la dislocation des dois de la main	on the dislocation of the fingers of the hand
Aucune fois sont desaluez li doi de la main a chescune part, aucune fois au dos de la palme ou au ventre;	never should the two sides of the hand, or the back of the palm or the stomach, be dislocated.
adonques estent le doi, et boute la dislocation a tes pouchés tant qu’il reviegne, puis sostien lou chief dou doi, et le pent vers la partie ou il est desjoins;	Then they should hold, and reduce the dislocation in their hands until it returns, then support the head with both hands, and align it towards the part where it is separated.
et le laisse II jors, et puis le met igal celui jor;	and leave it for two days, then set it equal again on the third day;
et de nut le lie, si com nos avons dit, et lou deslie de jor, et lou fai movoir, et le relie la nut;	and do not tie it, as we have said, but loosen it on the third day and make it move, then relive it with the nut.
et fai ce sovent, tant qu’il soit estroit, et tout ausi fai, se il est desaluez au ventre de la main, et fai si com tu as fait ci devant, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do this often, as long as it is tight, and do the same if it becomes distorted in the palm of the hand, and proceed as you have done before, until it is healed.
et tout ausi fai, quant il est desaluez d’autre part.	and do the same when it is dislocated from another side.
dou desaluement de l’eschinee dou dos	dislocation of the shoulder blade
Quant l’eschinee dou dos ou dou col est desaluee, ou il en i a plusors desaluees, si n’i a point de cure, car li mors haste le malaide.	When the shoulder blade or collarbone is dislocated and there is no cure, the patient faces a greater risk of death due to haste.
Et li signes si est que li egestions saut fuer sens volunteit, ne ne la puet tenir, et maintes fois sont mollifiez aucun membre, ou les II cuixes ou li dui bras ou I.	And the signs of this are that the patient's movements are sudden and involuntary, they cannot hold it, and often the limb becomes limp, whether it is one knee or both, or both arms.
Et maintes fois se muet li eschinee a IIII pars;	And often the elderly become mute, at least partially.
celle qui se muet au derrier si est apelee «gilbositez»:	the one who becomes mute at the back is called "gibbosity
li cure si est que tu rewarde se li gilbositez est venue d’enfance:	The cure is that you warm the joint if the stiffness comes from childhood.
si n’i ait point de cure ne de sanation dou tot.	If there is no cure or remedy for it at all.
Et celle que vient de cheoir ou de percussions ou de semblans choses, dirent li ancien manieres de cures par grans paroles, ou il n’a mie en toutes grant profit;	And that which comes from falling or impacts or similar things, they speak of ancient ways of cure with great words, but these have little to no benefit at all.
mais je l’ai abregiet selonc mon entention, et ai formez estrumens en diverses manieres.	But I have abreviate it according to my understanding, and formed instruments in various ways.
Je dis que en la gilbositeit que vient au pis devant, nen a engien ne santeit;	I say that in the gigot (fatty tissue) that comes to the foot first, no one has ever felt well.
et ausi cele que vient droitement en II costez, et ne puet on curer fuers que celi proprement qui vient au dos, si com je dis;	and also those that come straight to the second side, and one cannot cure anything outside of that which comes properly to the back, as I say.
et est que li malaides soit estendus sus sa faice en I leu igal, et ait de l’estrain desoz lui, qu’il ne se blece;	and it is that the patient should be extended on their back equally in the first position, and have strain from below, so that they do not bend.
puis fiche I tison au chief en terre forment, et I autre as piez, et lie un liien pardesoz les asseles dou malaide, et I autre as hainches, et as genous, et as chevilles;	then insert a thorn into the ground at the head, and another under, and tie a string from below around the patient's limbs, and another at the hips, and at the thighs, and at the ankles.
et dui ministre saichent les liiens, li uns au chief et li autres as piez, parmi les II tisons;	and two attendants know the ligaments, one at the head and the other at the foot, among the two splints.
et soient bien fermez, li tison si com nos avons dit, et li mires mette ses paumes sus l’espinee forment, tant qu’ele reviegne.	and they should be well secured; the splint as we have said, and the surgeon places his palms on the protruding bone, until it heals.
Et s’elle ne revient par ceste cure, si pren une tauble de III bras de lonc, et chevé desoz la paroit, et li malaides soit en costé, et boute le chief de la tauble desoz la paroit, puis met le mileu de la tauble sus l’espinee;	And if it does not heal with this treatment, take a table three feet long, cut a slot in the wall, and place the patient on their side, then turn the head of the table away from the wall, and put the middle part of the table over the bone.
et mette li mires ses piez sus l’autre chief de la tauble, et presse bien, tant qu’il reviegne au leu;	and place the mirror on the other side of the table, and press firmly until it returns to its place.
et se tu vues, si le fai au tornet qui torne a la main.	and if you look, do it with the turning wheel that turns in your hand.
Et est que tu fiches II tisons au chief dou malaide d’un bras de grant, et devers les piez II autres, et ait entre chescun tison, desoure et desoz, une paume d’espaice de lonc;	And take two sharp splints from a large limb of a patient and place them at the head of the dislocated arm, then put your other hands on top, with one palm-length space between each splint.
et ait en chescun tison I pertus, ou li tornet corre, et soient li tison fermement en terre, si qu’il ne se muevent;	and make each splint have a hole, or let the turning wheel run through them, and ensure the splints are firmly in place so they do not move.
et entre chescuns II tisons ait I tison tornant, sor coi li liien tornent, et ait en II tornans II petis tisons d’une paume de lonc, por torner le tornet;	and between each of the two pieces there should be one piece that turns, so that the joint is restored, and it has two small pieces turning in one hand, to return to its original position.
et puis lie lou lien qui est parmi les asseles au tornet devers le chief, et l’autre liien devers les piez a l’autre tornet, et chescuns des ministres torne son tornet a tout le liien, et li maistres mette l’espinee igal si com nos avons dit.	and then tie the ligament that is among the attached to the joint towards the top, and the other ligament towards the foot to the other joint, and each of the assistants turns their joint with the entire ligament, and the master sets the splint evenly as we have said.
Et quant elle est igalz, si met sus emplaustre desiccatif avec abun d’uef, et puis les estoupes, et puis l’estele d’une tablete de III dois de lonc, que porpreigne lou leu de la gilbositeit et la partie de l’espondile sainne, puis le lie d’un liien, si com nos avons dit, et use li malaides de norrissement subtil, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when it is even, apply a drying plaster with plenty of heat, then the pads, and then the plank of three fingers in length, which secures the joint from the stiffness and the healthy part of the spine, then tie it with a ligament as we have said, and use gentle treatment for the patient until it is healed.
et s’aucune chose vient en la fin de la santez, si covient aministrer medicines amollissans et asouajans, avec l’estele que nos avons dit ci devant;	and if any thing comes to the end of health, it is necessary to administer soft and soothing medicines, with the care that we have said above;
et aucune fois i aministre on une piece de plonc, et aucune fois vient li apparance en la derriere spondile dou dos, et cuide on que ce soit dislocations;	and never administer a plug, and never does the appearance come in the last spine of the back, and it is believed that this is a dislocation;
et c’est li os qui apert, por coi on n’i doit mie avoir presumption:	and it is the bone that opens, so one must not have presumption;
par aventure feroit venir la mort.	in case death were to come.
des dislocations de la hainche	Of dislocations of the spine
Saiches que as jointures de la hainche et as jointures de l’espaule ne vient fuers que dislocacions soulement, ne n’i vient mie si com as autres jointures;	You know that the joints of the spine and the joints of the shoulder only cause dislocations, not like the other joints.
et li jointure de la hainche est desaluee selonc IIII parties:	and the spinal joint is misaligned according to three parts:
dedens et defuer ,et devant et derrier;	inside, outside, front, and back;
et plus dedens c’aillors, et poc desalue devant et derrier.	and more inside, then slightly misaligned in front and back.
Et li conoissance de sa dislocations dedens si est que quant on joint la jambe malaide avec la sainne, si est plus longe, et apert plus li malaides genous que li sains, et ne puet li malaides doubler son genoil au feu;	And the knowledge of his dislocation is such that when you join the diseased leg with the healthy one, it extends further, and opens up the diseased knees more widely than the healthy ones, and the patient cannot bend their knee fully.
et est li leus qui est delez enflez d’aposteme chaut, por ceu que li chiés de la cuixe vient lai.	and it is the swelling that is affected by hot abscess, because the joint of the thigh comes over here.
Et li signe de celui cui il vient au defuer, si est que cist accident sont contraire a ces devant.	And the sign of him who experiences this at death is that this event is contrary to what has been said before.
Et li signes de celui cui avient au devant, si est qu’il estent bien sa jambe selonc l’acomplissement;	And the signs of one who experiences it in front, are that their leg is straight according to its natural position;
toutevoie, ne double mie le genoil sens dolor, et s’on le vuet faire aler, si ne puet avant, et retient son urine, et enfle li angre, et quant il vait, si passe sus le talon.	but do not bend the knee without pain, and if you want to make it move, it cannot go forward, and it retains urine, and swells up the ankle, and when it moves, it goes over the heel.
Et li signes de celui cui il avient derrier, si est qu’il ne puet espandre son genoil, ne doubler, et est celle jambe plus torte de l’autre, et li angre est mollifié, et est li chiés de la cuixe au leu desoz les costes.	And the signs of him who experiences this afterward, are that he cannot spread or bend his knee, and one leg is more twisted than the other, and the angre is softened, and the limb of the thigh is raised on the side of the ribs.
Li ramenemens de ceste semblance de dislocation si est que tu rewarde se li dislocations est anciainne, et elle demore selonc sa disposition, si n’i a nule cure;	They must reset this appearance of dislocation if it is old and persists according to its nature, as there is no cure for it.
et n’i covient mie qu’il ait presumption.	and there should be no presumption that it will not recur.
Et en celi dont li dislocation est fresche, et c’est des IIII manieres de dislocation, si te haste que tu tornes la jointe, et l’esten dedens et defuer, et la muef a destre et senestre;	And for the one whose dislocation is recent, there are three types of dislocation: if you hurry to return the joint, it will be inside and outside, or moved to the right or left.
par aventure si revenra, et n’a mestier d’autre cure.	for fear it may return, and there needs be no other cure.
Et s’il ne revient en ceste maniere, si covient que tu apareilles I ministre fort, et esten la jambe fort a II mains, ou a I liien que soit liiez sus lou genoil;	And if it does not return in this manner, then you must prepare a strong compress and extend the leg firmly at two hands, or fasten it to the knee joint.
et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe;	and other ministers extend their hand over it in such a way that they press their hands down on the sore spots, then pull firmly with a slow motion on the leg just above the ankle.
et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien;	and another holds the head with a firm grip.
et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	and they stretch up and down several times, until the patient is raised from the ground once, and remains still.
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as IIII semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	This method of extension is common to all three cases, and if the dislocation returns, as we have said, it is good.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance.	If this is not done, then care must be taken of its appearance.
Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;	When dislocation occurs in the joints, it is necessary that you bring the patient to rest on their healthy side, then wrap a bandage around the root of the thigh, and the joint that is away from the pain, then stretch the bandage upwards towards the pain and downwards towards the stronger part.
puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment:	then apply pressure with your hands on the patient's arms, embrace the large joint of the affected thigh, and stretch it to a wide angle.
si revenra a son leu maintenant;	if it returns to its place now;
et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	and this method of dislocation is lighter than others.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres;	And if you cannot hold it in that way as we have said, then you should tie the two feet of the patient together with a strong, soft ligature on the two heels and on the two knees, and let the injured leg be extended two more degrees than the other.
puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc;	then it should be hung on a pole with the head down, and two long arms above the ground.
puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	then instruct the assistant to embrace the hip joint, and have other assistants with the patient who are embracing the hip, for the joints will now heal slowly.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	And when the dislocation is external, if the patient lies down, as we have said in the case of stiffness, and carefully extracts the ligament from the affected leg, also from the opposite side;
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	then place two splints, one at the hip and another below, then insert a splint between the hips of the patient in the shape of a bow.
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	and place moist rags around it, so the patient does not suffer pain, then extend each limb towards him and equally apply the medication to the dislocation.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	If it returns, it is good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If it does not return, place it on a table and press it as we have said in the previous section, and lay the patient on their healthy side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	And when the dislocation is present, it is necessary to extend the affected leg forcibly, as I have said before.
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	and apply the compress to his pain of being on the affected limb, then press with the other hand and stretch it downwards towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	And if the dislocation is on the outside, it is not necessary to stretch the affected limb downwards or lift it up, but rather, it should be held in the same position as when the hip was dislocated, as we have gently described above.
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	and place it on his face, with the limb extended as we have said before, and all must press down on the joint on the table;
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	and it will be clear when the patient extends his legs, and they will be even.
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	then tighten the thighs, and apply the plaster, and wrap it with a bandage, so that the hip does not move.
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	and rest for three or four days, then untie it, and apply the plaster again.
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	and if you see that they are even, hold them as before, and leave it for three days.
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	then dislocate it again, and make it go smoothly, as long as the limb is comfortable.
de la dislocation dou genoil	From the dislocation of the knee.
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	The dislocation is treated according to three methods:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	that is to say, internally and externally, and behind.
et ne desalue point devant.	and do not treat it in front.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the sign is that you instruct the patient to bend their leg at the knee, and if it does not return to its place at the knee, know that it is dislocated.
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	and the restoration of all is that you make the patient sit upright, and extend their leg if they can, and place them face down on your lap, and rest their foot on top of yours.
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	then take their kneecap in your palms, pull it between your fingers, then bend both sides of the knee cap;
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	and other helpers extend their help until the knee returns to its place, and the sign is that it has recovered well its leg slightly.
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	and apply a poultice, and make the leg recover to its place, and hold it together tightly for three or four days, then release it.
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	and the patients should not move about until the limb is healed.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limb is not in place, apply firm extension as we have said in the treatment of the shoulder, until it is healed.
de la dislocation dou talon	of the dislocation of the heel
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heels are neither completely dislocated nor fully aligned, and they are distorted both inwardly and outwardly.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	And the sign of this is that the ankle is swollen, and it turns red at the site where it was dislocated.
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	We reset it if it is slight, and one must gently extend their hands when they are slightly dislocated.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	And when it is slightly dislocated, one should make the patient lie straight and hold them by the leg above the ankle with a helper.
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	then take the foot in your right hand, and then with your left hand twice, then extend it upwards, and gently pull the foot upwards.
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	and do this twice as we have said, by extending and pulling the foot.
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	If it returns, that's good.
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	If it does not return, the work must be restarted, for it returns.
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	and if it cannot return in that way, lay the patient on their back on the ground, and insert a stick firmly into the earth between their legs, and wrap cloth around them to prevent the patient from hurting themselves.
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	then strike the patient's thigh, and another assistant extends the leg or holds it at the knee;
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	then extend each limb equally, and the bands should be placed again between the legs of the patient to hold the patient still when pulled.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	then place the mirrors equally on the dislocation of his hands, and another minister ties the healthy leg at the ankle, and the dislocation will return steadily.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	And when it has healed somewhat, apply the plaster and fill it up, and stretch it tightly, and fasten the foot to the leg, and hold the reins that are on the ankle behind, so that the bandages are not too tight.
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	then leave it for two or three days, and gently move it if it is strained.
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	then dislocate it on the third or fourth day, and make sure the patient walks for three days.
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	and if it does not heal by this time, it is not fortunate that it will still be dislocated.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if abscesses form, it is necessary to soothe them, as we have said elsewhere, while they are clean.
des dois	Of the two (parts/sides)
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When both (sides) are dislocated, if they need to be realigned without effort, it is a light task.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocation is in any other part of the foot or leg, it is necessary that you make the patient lie on his back or on a table with his body straight, and place your foot on what opens up from these joints, then press gently with your foot until it returns.
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	and when they are even and open nothing, place the sole of the foot on a table with two joints, then stretch it firm and leave it for three days, then loosen it.
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and make it rest until it is healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	From wound and dislocation together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When a wound comes with a dislocation and one wants to restore it, often the patient dies.
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	if you are not presumptuous in treatment, since you are ignorant of the art and have not practiced it for long, and if you lack compassion and mercy and are slow to act, do not be bold.
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	and at the beginning of things, apply hot poultices to the abscess, and leave the patient in God's hands, if you have no hope for healing.
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	and if you see hope, then now reset the member to its place, so that the abscesses heat goes away;
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	and when the member is in place, apply hot poultices to the abscesses, and treat the wound as appropriate, with dried herbs.
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	and if with the dislocation there is a fracture, and small bones are broken, then as we have said in simple illnesses:
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	and keep from entering a path of fear, according to what I have said, for it is your movement according to your Creator, and for the knowledge of your arms and body.
